Second Son

Construction and Use of Copper Roller Printing Machine 172

— Rui Yu-cheng

A Scotsman named Bell first invented this copper roller printing machine in 1783. Two years later, he implemented this business in factories. Through years of machine improvements and scientific advancements, it has been gradually removed and renewed, resulting in today's achievements. Although it cannot be said that it has reached the pinnacle, it can be called perfect. So what does the latest modern printing machine look like? I will briefly explain its structure as follows:

It is roughly a hollow copper roller with engraved patterns on it, set on the outside of an iron shaft: a large iron roller rests on top of the copper roller: a brush rests below, and a paint tray supports the brush below. The tray contains paint: a part of the bottom of the brush is immersed in the paint: a sharp blade leans diagonally in the center of the copper roller. The copper roller rotates, and the paint is applied to the copper roller. After being scraped by the blade, the paint on the flat surface of the copper roller is completely scraped off. The engraved part is recessed and does not touch the scraper, so only the paint remains inside the engraved part: the outside of the large iron roller is surrounded by layers of wool felt, and the tightly pressed copper roller below gains elastic force: the outside of the wool felt is covered with a layer of wool lining felt or rubber cloth, so that the elastic properties are extra increased: the outside of the wool lining felt is covered with cotton lining cloth to protect the wool lining felt so that it is not touched and soiled by the paint on the copper roller: the outside of the cotton lining cloth is where the fabric to be printed is placed. When the machine is turned on, the paint on the copper roller, after being scraped by the blade, is left in the recessed area where it has been engraved, and the fabric to be printed on the outside of the large iron roller is pressed on top: relying on the elasticity of the wool felt in the middle: the carved pattern is printed on the fabric in the same pattern.

The entire printing machine is driven by a motor or water tank: when the large gear disc rotates, the small gear disc inlaid on the right end of the iron shaft above also moves, and at the same time, the gear disc on the left end of the iron shaft rotates the gear disc of the brush below. The paint in the disc follows the rotation of the brush, turning up and sticking to the top of the copper roller. The large iron shaft above also starts to rotate due to the pressure of the copper roller below. This endless mutual rotation prints fabrics with various patterns and designs. Science is truly omnipotent!

Social Improvement Discussion Group

Love's Pain and Nerve Relations 173

— A Reader

Page 20

Because people's hearts are different, each as unique as their faces, the truth of love is different for everyone. According to people with experience, the crystallization of true love is due to the union of spirit and flesh. The symbol of love can be divided into two sections using anatomical methods:

One, tangible love: People are spiritual animals, and inevitably have emotions: Since God has endowed people with a kind of emotion, then, it is easy to fall in love when encountering a suitable opposite sex. The joy between men and women, the beating of two hearts, forms a reluctant appearance. Over time, "headache," "fever," "vomiting," "sleepiness," "cramps," and other states follow the process of love and change in a thousand ways. Because this kind of morbid state can be diagnosed, it is called tangible love (Love Visible).

Two, intangible love: In other words, love is actually a mental illness. Or it can be said that it is the result of the nervous system being affected. In addition to the tendency of the spirit, there is also the requirement of the flesh. Because the nervous system is the hub of the brain (referring to the spirit) and the sexual organs (referring to the flesh), there is a close relationship. The soul constantly thinks, the body keeps burning, and the fire of love burns from the head to the eyes, and from the eyes to the whole body. So some people say that love and death are equally great | If there is no ability to control oneself, in the tragedy of unrequited love, the man will go crazy, and the woman will go silly, and even urgently take the path of suicide. Nervous breakdown, nervous abnormality, nervous abnormality are such painful things in the world! Because thoughts cannot be concentrated, and there is no medicine to cure mental illness, it is called intangible love (Love Invisible).

The pain and nerve influence of love are as described above, and from this we can further extend the magical power of love to society. The influence of love can make a robber who murders and arson improve and become a virtuous gentleman: Conversely, the damage of love can make a virtuous gentleman angry and do things that kill and bleed. Therefore, this new term 丨 love 丨 not only contains sociality, but also contains transformative, and has become an extremely serious problem in modern times. In history, in movies, in novels, I don't know how many times it has been performed. Recently, the love murder case between Ms. Tao Sijin and Sister Li is an example. Of course, love does not allow the intervention of a third party. They have their inside story, and I as the author have no right to interfere: But I myself am a part of society, and I have to think of some ways to improve it: How to increase the happiness of the crowd and reduce the pain of love?

I think my way is, one, to strive hard to make lovers become relatives: two, to believe in religion, to stabilize the soul and not to fall: three, to overcome desires with righteousness: to restrain emotions with reason: there are many good men and beautiful women in the world, and you can find another good couple. Four, thinking should be lofty, and vision should be broad: Although love is not successful, you can still do other work that is beneficial to the world. Sacrificing the small self to become the big self is not worthy of being a hero or heroine. Finally, let the author copy the teachings of the French General Foch to encourage general modern youths:

"Men should do more work: women should do more praying." Keep your own peace, complete your personality. School Portrait

The Price of a Kiss 174

Liu Ying

This afternoon, the geography teacher from 1 to 2 took leave. But the notice was posted late, and the students were already waiting in the classroom. S and D stood at the classroom door, craning their necks, waiting for the echo of the classmate who went to inquire about the news. After a while, this scout jumped back with good news and said that the leave slip had been posted. At this point, the entire classroom exploded like soda bubbles rising from a bottle cap, with cheers, applause, laughter, and the sound of feet hitting the ground with stools all at once. Then groups of students, talking and laughing with books in hand, walked out of the classroom.

"Let's go eat ice cream!" S shouted from behind, calling out to D, who was heading out of the classroom door. D responded with a "yes," and turned the toes of his feet, which were originally turning right to go to the dormitory, 180 degrees and went with S.

Miss C, who loves quiet and not movement, was taking a class in this classroom in the next hour. One reason was to save running back and forth, and the other reason was that she saw other classmates all leaving, leaving only her alone. She just sat there quietly and read a book.

It was very hot. On the open space next to the classroom, there were usually several male students playing small leather balls, but now they were also driven away by the scorching sun. The surrounding air was unusually silent. Inside the classroom, only the sound of Miss C turning the pages of her book could be heard about every few minutes. But after half an hour, the sound of turning pages also stopped. Miss C fell asleep on the table.

S and D came back from a cold food store at the school gate. Just as they walked to the window of a classroom facing the corridor, S pulled D's arm, and the two stopped at the same time. D glanced at S, and then looked at the place indicated by S's pointed mouth.

"Miss C!" D was both surprised and happy.

"The sleeping face of a female student! It's rare to see!"

"Let's go in and have a good look!"

"I agree!"

The two entered the classroom quietly and walked close to Miss C.

D stared at Miss C's mouth for a long time. Miss C's lips twitched nervously. D said with an envious tone, "I don't know who will be lucky enough to get it in the future!"

"Isn't it easy to kiss? Now is an opportunity, anyway, she won't notice."

"Hmph, if you dare to kiss her, I'll treat you to ten cups of ice cream." "Really," I bet you don't dare. "Ten cups of ice cream have to count!" "Count."

S made up his mind, walked lightly to Miss C, bent down and carefully kissed Miss C's lips, but before S could lift his head, Miss C had woken up. She quickly wiped her mouth with a handkerchief like a reflex action, and angrily asked S, "What are you doing?"

"There was a fly on your lips? I:::" S himself felt that this answer was too weak, and couldn't help but laugh out loud. D also couldn't help but laugh loudly.

Miss C felt even more insulted by their laughter, and she threw herself on the table and cried loudly.

S and D looked at each other, everyone stuck out their tongues.

At this time, the end of class bell rang, and the students rushed over to see the show. S was afraid that the situation would escalate, and repeatedly said sorry to Miss C, but Miss C ignored him, stood up, covered her face with one hand, and cried out of the classroom. The classmates asked S and D one after another what was going on, but their answers were always "nothing."

The situation finally escalated. Miss C didn't go to class and cried on the bed in the dormitory. She refused to eat dinner. The female classmate in the same room reported it to the resident supervisor. The resident supervisor came to the girls' dormitory to ask, but Miss C didn't answer a single word.

All the male students in the school were discussing and speculating about the cause of the incident. Later, a rumor spread that S and D had committed violence against Miss C in a certain classroom, causing Miss C to have a bitter pill that she couldn't swallow.

S saw that the students' speculation exceeded his criminal behavior, and he was afraid that the school authorities would hear about it, which would be even more detrimental to him. He had to bravely go to the academic affairs office to confess. Of course, he added many words to defend himself, but he honestly confessed the fact of kissing.

The Dean of Academic Affairs thought very highly of the confession, so he advocated punishing S lightly, but because the class supervisor opposed it, the result was a compromise with a short notice posted.

S's insult to a female student will be recorded with a major demerit. Academic Affairs Office

Later, a male student criticized on the bulletin board:

"The price of a female student's kiss is only a major demerit, and there are ten cups of ice cream to eat! Worth it, worth it."

Bloodiness

A Letter Filled with Loving Blood 175

Man Qian

Dearest Sister G:

Sister G, our army at noon today has advanced to a valley only thirty or forty li away from City C. We are preparing to attack the city at dawn tomorrow, to recover my City C, which has been under the iron heel for nearly a year. Some of my brothers are writing letters, others are flexing their muscles, preparing for the fierce battle tomorrow. I am taking this opportunity to pick up my pen and talk to you, whom I haven't seen for over a month. I imagine you must be eagerly waiting for this!

Thinking of the past, it truly makes me extremely sad. But, separations in life are inevitable, especially since I am doing this to protect my country and fight my enemies. G! Do you remember, the day before I left home, I usually returned home around four o'clock in the afternoon after school, and at home, we would laugh and talk, but I had never been as late as eleven o'clock at night. This alone was enough to surprise you and my loving parents.

Then, seeing my face, full of hot blood and excitement, coupled with a sad expression due to the impending departure, when you heard me say "Your son has joined the volunteer army...", you were all simply stunned. Your eyes, I saw, were red, and in an instant, you covered your face and ran upstairs.

At this time, only Father, Mother, and I remained. Finally, Father broke the silence and said: "Hua'er! You must understand clearly, we are not used to life in the army. Indeed, everyone has the responsibility to love and save the country, but saving the country doesn't necessarily mean taking up a gun and fighting the enemy! The rear needs us even more, Hua'er! Listen to your father's words, I beg you..."

Father is an elderly man and cannot speak continuously for long. He had only said a few words and was already out of breath. Ah! I truly appreciate Father and deeply understand his good intentions, pitying his son's weak body, unable to endure the life in the military camp. At the same time, Mother was also saying through tears:

"Hua'er! It hasn't been easy raising you to this age. Once you leave your aging and sickly parents and your gentle and considerate wife, how can we bear it? Think about it, your father is old and useless, and I am just like this old woman, bedridden every other day. Your wife is already three months pregnant. If you leave us now to go to that bloody battlefield, what if something goes wrong? Who will we rely on?... Hua'er!"

Mother's words were filled with grief and she couldn't speak clearly. I couldn't help but cry in response. At the same time, I seemed to hear a very faint sobbing coming from upstairs. At this time, my heart was at war. "Go"? "Don't go"? But in the end, I firmly believed that the only way to find a way out for our country was through armed resistance, to go to the front line to kill enemies and sacrifice myself. Therefore, I still insisted on my opinion and resolutely replied with a "No."

It had been long past one o'clock. Father felt that there was no room for further persuasion. Finally, he said, "It's late, go upstairs and sleep. Are our words well-intentioned or malicious? Think about it carefully."

Without answering, I hesitated and walked into the room, seeing that you were not asleep, your eyes were red and swollen like walnuts. I really couldn't think of any words to comfort you. I just busied myself tidying up everything I needed, preparing to leave on time in the morning. Seeing me in this busy state, you must have been even more surprised, right? Otherwise, how could you ask me, "What are you doing? Are you leaving us tomorrow?" Ah! You cried softly. At this time, I didn't know what to do, except to hold you tightly, kiss you sweetly. It was only with great difficulty that you stopped crying and asked me, with a mix of resentment and sorrow, the reason for abandoning the family and going far away. I then told you about the oppression of the neighbor to the east, the decline of the country, the responsibilities of a citizen, and that my reason for leaving home was to find a way out for the country and seek survival for the nation. Who knew that you were also a woman with a heart full of passion? After hearing my words, you actually changed your overly sentimental attitude and even encouraged me with words, helping me pack my bags.

G! At this time, how happy I was in my heart! I couldn't help but give you another sweet and long kiss.

Sister G: Now, I'm making you tired, having to take care of family affairs, serve elderly parents, and being pregnant. Ah! I have nothing else to repay you with now. Every corner of this letter has been kissed by me. Now I send it to you, please savor it carefully! At the same time, I hope to kill a few more enemies tomorrow to comfort my soulmate. Goodbye, dear sister, your loving Hua on the day before the fierce battle.
